An older but still valuable introduction to existentialism is [3mIrrational Man: A Study in Existential Philosophy [0mby William Barrett 
(New York: Anchor Books, 1962, 2nd edn. 1990). Two helpful collections of writings by leading existentialist authors are [3m

Reader: An Anthology of Key Texts [0m, ed. Paul S. MacDonald (New York: Routledge, 2001). Someone wishing to pursue essays on the 
basic concepts of existential and phenomenological thought by a variety of authors, as well as existential and phenomenological 
contributions to a number of topics in current philosophical discussion should consult Hubert L. Dreyfus and Mark A. Wrathall 
(eds.), [3mA Companion to Existentialism and Phenomenology [0m(Oxford: Blackwell, 2006). 

Chapter-length essays on existentialism, phenomenology, and most of the individual philosophers discussed here, along with helpful 
suggestions for further reading, are available in the [3mStanford Encyclopedia of Philosophy [0m, online at [3mhttp://plato.stanford.edu. [0m
Relevant essays on individual philosophers can be found in [3mThe Macmillan Encyclopedia of Philosophy [0m, 2nd edn. (Farmington Hills, 
MI: Thomson Gale, 2006); [3mThe Routledge History of Philosophy [0m, especially vol. 7, [3mThe Nineteenth Century [0m, ed. C. L. Ten, and vol. 
8, [3mContinental Philosophy in the 20th Century [0m, ed. Richard Kearney (London: Routledge, 1994); [3mThe Edinburgh Encyclopedia of 
Continental Philosophy [0m, ed. Simon Glendinning (Edinburgh: Edinburgh University Press, 1999); and [3mA Companion to Continental 
Philosophy [0m, ed. Simon Critchley and William Schroeder (Oxford: Blackwell, 1998). 

[1mุงููุตู ุงูุฃูู: ุงูููุณูุฉ ูุฃุณููุจ ุญูุงุฉ [0m

Those interested in this topic might consult Pierre Hadot, [3mWhat is Ancient Philosophy? [0m(Cambridge, MA: Harvard University Press,

Penguin, 2004) and Franz Kafkaโs [3mThe Trial [0m(New York: Schocken Books, 1998), or its film version by Orson Welles (1963) with

(Cambridge: Cambridge University Press, 1999). 

[1mุงููุตู ุงูุซุงูู: ุงูุชุญูู ุฅูู ุงููุฑุฏูุฉ [0m

[1mุงููุตู ุงูุซุงูุซ: ุงูููุณูุฉ ุงูุฅูุณุงููุฉ: ูุง ููุง ููุง ุนูููุง [0m

A valuable overview is Jacob Golombโs [3mIn Search of Authenticity: From Kierkegaard to Camus [0m(London: Routledge, 1995). [3mThe Ethics

[1mุงููุตู ุงูุฎุงูุณ: ูุฑุฏูุฉ ููุจูุชุฉุ ุงููุฌูุฏูุฉ ูุงูููุฑ ุงูุงุฌุชูุงุนู [0m

De Beauvoirโs autobiography, especially [3mForce of Circumstance [0m, covering 1944โ62 (New York: Putnam, 1965), and [3mAll Said and Done [0m,
